Callers must ensure external synchronization\n * or create separate instances if multiple threads need concurrent access. However, since batches are\n * typically read-only after creation, sharing immutable batch instances across threads is safe.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Binary Format:</b> The v2 record batch consists of a fixed header (56 bytes) followed by\n * variable-length record data. The CRC covers all bytes after the magic byte, including attributes,\n * timestamps, producer IDs, sequence numbers, and record data. The partition leader epoch is\n * intentionally excluded from the CRC to allow brokers to update it in-place without recomputation.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Schema:</b>\n * <pre>{@code\n *   RecordBatch =>\n *     BaseOffset => Int64\n *     Length => Int32\n *     PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\n *     Magic => Int8\n *     CRC => Uint32\n *     Attributes => Int16\n *     LastOffsetDelta => Int32\n *     BaseTimestamp => Int64\n *     MaxTimestamp => Int64\n *     ProducerId => Int64\n *     ProducerEpoch => Int16\n *     BaseSequence => Int32\n *     RecordsCount => Int32\n *     Records => [Record]\n * }</pre>\n * </p>\n *\n * <p><b>Compression:</b> When compression is enabled, the compressed record data immediately\n * follows the record count field. Decompression is handled transparently by {@link #streamingIterator}\n * and related methods.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Compaction Behavior:</b> During log compaction, the base and last offsets/sequences are\n * preserved from the original batch to maintain producer state integrity. This ensures that after\n * a broker restart, the producer's expected next sequence number remains in sync with the broker's\n * state, preventing spurious OutOfOrderSequence errors.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Attributes:</b> The 16-bit attributes field encodes compression type, timestamp type,\n * transactional flag, control flag, and delete horizon flag. The upper 10 bits are currently unused\n * and must be zero for forward compatibility.</p>\n *\n * @see RecordBatch\n * @see MutableRecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecords\n */\npublic class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch implements MutableRecordBatch {\n    // Field offset constants for binary format layout\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET = 0;\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int LENGTH_OFFSET = BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET + BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH;\n    static final int LENGTH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET = LENGTH_OFFSET + LENGTH_LENGTH;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int MAGIC_OFFSET = PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAGIC_LENGTH = 1;\n    public static final int CRC_OFFSET = MAGIC_OFFSET + MAGIC_LENGTH;\n    static final int CRC_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET = CRC_OFFSET + CRC_LENGTH;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH = 2;\n    public static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET = ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET + ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH;\n    static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET = MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET = PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET + PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 2;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET = PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH = 4;\n    public static final int RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET = BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET + BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH;\n    static final int RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int RECORDS_OFFSET = RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET + RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH;\n    public static final int RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD = RECORDS_OFFSET;\n\n    // Attribute bit masks\n    private static final byte COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK = 0x07;\n    private static final byte TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK = 0x10;\n    private static final int CONTROL_FLAG_MASK = 0x20;\n    private static final byte DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK = 0x40;\n    private static final byte TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK = 0x08;\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    /**\n     * Construct a {@code DefaultRecordBatch} wrapping the given buffer.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> The caller is responsible for ensuring that the buffer\n     * is not modified concurrently while this batch is in use.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer A {@link ByteBuffer} positioned at the start of a magic v2 batch.\n     *               The buffer must contain at least {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes\n     *               and remain valid for the lifetime of this batch instance.\n     */\n    DefaultRecordBatch(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public byte magic() {\n        return buffer.get(MAGIC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void ensureValid() {\n        if (sizeInBytes() < RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD)\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record batch is corrupt (the size \" + sizeInBytes() +\n                    \" is smaller than the minimum allowed overhead \" + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + \")\");\n\n        if (!isValid())\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record is corrupt (stored crc = \" + checksum()\n                    + \", computed crc = \" + computeChecksum() + \")\");\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Gets the base timestamp of the batch, which is used to calculate individual record timestamps\n     * by adding per-record timestamp deltas.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Semantics:</b>\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>If the batch is not empty: timestamp of the first record in the original batch</li>\n     *   <li>If the batch is empty: set to {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} (which is -1)</li>\n     *   <li>If delete horizon is set: the delete horizon timestamp (used during compaction)</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return The base timestamp in milliseconds since epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP}\n     *         if empty or not applicable\n     */\n    public long baseTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long maxTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TimestampType timestampType() {\n        return (attributes() & TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK) == 0 ? TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long baseOffset() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long lastOffset() {\n        return baseOffset() + lastOffsetDelta();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long producerId() {\n        return buffer.getLong(PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public short producerEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getShort(PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int baseSequence() {\n        return buffer.getInt(BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int lastOffsetDelta() {\n        return buffer.getInt(LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int lastSequence() {\n        int baseSequence = baseSequence();\n        if (baseSequence == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n            return RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE;\n        return incrementSequence(baseSequence, lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CompressionType compressionType() {\n        return CompressionType.forId(attributes() & COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return LOG_OVERHEAD + buffer.getInt(LENGTH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int count() {\n        return buffer.getInt(RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Integer countOrNull() {\n        return count();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch to the given buffer without decompression.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance:</b> This is a zero-copy operation that uses a buffer duplicate.\n     * If the batch is compressed, the compressed data is written as-is.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}; must have at least\n     *               {@link #sizeInBytes()} remaining bytes\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        buffer.put(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch to the given stream.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance:</b> This operation may be more efficient than {@link #writeTo(ByteBuffer)}\n     * for certain {@link ByteBufferOutputStream} implementations that support bulk writes.</p>\n     *\n     * @param outputStream The destination {@link ByteBufferOutputStream}; must have capacity\n     *                     for at least {@link #sizeInBytes()} bytes\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBufferOutputStream outputStream) {\n        outputStream.write(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isTransactional() {\n        return (attributes() & TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    private boolean hasDeleteHorizonMs() {\n        return (attributes() & DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs() {\n        if (hasDeleteHorizonMs())\n            return OptionalLong.of(buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET));\n        else\n            return OptionalLong.empty();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isControlBatch() {\n        return (attributes() & CONTROL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int partitionLeaderEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create an input stream for reading the serialized record data of this batch.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Compression Handling:</b> If the batch is compressed, the returned stream\n     * automatically decompresses data as it is read. The decompression is performed using\n     * the compression type specified in the batch attributes and the provided buffer supplier.</p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier of {@link ByteBuffer}s for decompression buffers.\n     *                       For optimal performance, the supplier should reuse buffers across calls.\n     * @return An {@link InputStream} positioned at the start of the records section.\n     *         For compressed batches, the stream wraps a decompression wrapper.\n     */\n    public InputStream recordInputStream(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return Compression.of(compressionType()).build().wrapForInput(buffer, magic(), bufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> compressedIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier, boolean skipKeyValue) {\n        final InputStream inputStream = recordInputStream(bufferSupplier);\n\n        if (skipKeyValue) {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readPartiallyFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        } else {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        }\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> uncompressedIterator() {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return new RecordIterator() {\n            @Override\n            protected Record readNext(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) {\n                try {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(buffer, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                } catch (BufferUnderflowException e) {\n                    throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Incorrect declared batch size, premature EOF reached\");\n                }\n            }\n            @Override\n            protected boolean ensureNoneRemaining() {\n                return !buffer.hasRemaining();\n            }\n            @Override\n            public void close() {}\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return an iterator over records in this batch, decompressing if necessary.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Compression Handling:</b> If the batch is compressed, this method fully decompresses\n     * the record stream into memory before returning an iterator. This approach trades memory for\n     * simplicity and resource safety (the returned iterator does not need to be closed).\n     * For memory-constrained scenarios, prefer {@link #streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)}.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Empty Batches:</b> If the batch contains no records, returns an empty iterator.</p>\n     *\n     * @return An {@link Iterator} over {@link Record}s; safe to use in enhanced for-loops\n     *         and does not require explicit closure\n     */\n    @Override\n    public Iterator<Record> iterator() {\n        if (count() == 0)\n            return Collections.emptyIterator();\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // for a normal iterator, we cannot ensure that the underlying compression stream is closed,\n        // so we decompress the full record set here. Use cases which call for a lower memory footprint\n        // can use `streamingIterator` at the cost of additional complexity\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = compressedIterator(BufferSupplier.NO_CACHING, false)) {\n            List<Record> records = new ArrayList<>(count());\n            while (iterator.hasNext())\n                records.add(iterator.next());\n            return records.iterator();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a closeable iterator that skips over record key/value/header data during iteration.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Use Case:</b> This is useful for operations that only need record metadata (offsets,\n     * timestamps, producer IDs) without the actual record content. This can significantly reduce\n     * memory usage and improve performance compared to fully reading every record.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance Note:</b>\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>For compressed batches: Uses a streaming decompression iterator with skipping enabled</li>\n     *   <li>For uncompressed batches: Falls back to normal iteration since skipping is less efficient\n     *       than just reading through the data</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier for decompression buffers if the batch is compressed\n     * @return A {@link CloseableIterator} over records with minimal data loading;\n     *         must be closed by the caller if the batch is compressed\n     */\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> skipKeyValueIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (count() == 0) {\n            return CloseableIterator.wrap(Collections.emptyIterator());\n        }\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // we define this to be a closable iterator so that caller (i.e. the log validator) needs to close it\n        // while we can save memory footprint of not decompressing the full record set ahead of time\n        return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, true);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return a streaming iterator for lazy decompression and record parsing.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Memory Efficiency:</b> For compressed batches, this iterator decompresses data\n     * on-demand as {@link Iterator#next()} is called, rather than loading the entire decompressed\n     * stream into memory. This is critical for memory-constrained scenarios or when processing\n     * large batches.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Resource Management:</b> The returned iterator must be explicitly closed\n     * (preferably via try-with-resources) to release decompression resources.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Buffer Supplier Recommendation:</b> Provide a {@link BufferSupplier} that\n     * reuses buffers across multiple iterations. This significantly improves performance\n     * by avoiding repeated allocations of large decompression buffers (e.g., 64 KB for LZ4).</p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier for decompression buffers. Suppliers that reuse\n     *                       buffers across calls have significant performance impact.\n     * @return A {@link CloseableIterator} that enables lazy decompression; must be closed by caller\n     */\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (isCompressed())\n            return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, false);\n        else\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Modify the last offset of this batch (as a mutable batch).\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> This method is <b>not thread-safe</b>. Concurrent calls to mutation\n     * methods or reads during mutation will produce undefined results.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>CRC Impact:</b> This method updates only the base offset to maintain the correct\n     * offset delta. The CRC remains valid since the offset fields are outside the CRC computation.</p>\n     *\n     * @param offset The new last offset for this batch; the base offset is automatically\n     *               adjusted to maintain the offset delta\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void setLastOffset(long offset) {\n        buffer.putLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, offset - lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Modify the maximum timestamp and timestamp type of this batch.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> This method is <b>not thread-safe</b>. Concurrent calls to mutation\n     * methods or reads during mutation will produce undefined results.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>CRC Recomputation:</b> If the timestamp or timestamp type changes, the CRC is\n     * automatically recomputed since both fields are covered by the checksum.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Optimization:</b> If the new values match the current ones, no modification occurs\n     * and CRC recomputation is skipped.</p>\n     *\n     * @param timestampType The new {@link TimestampType} for this batch\n     * @param maxTimestamp The new maximum timestamp in milliseconds since epoch\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType timestampType, long maxTimestamp) {\n        long currentMaxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        // We don't need to recompute crc if the timestamp is not updated.\n        if (timestampType() == timestampType && currentMaxTimestamp == maxTimestamp)\n            return;\n\n        byte attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType(), timestampType, isTransactional(), isControlBatch(), hasDeleteHorizonMs());\n        buffer.putShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        long crc = computeChecksum();\n        ByteUtils.writeUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET, crc);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set the partition leader epoch for this batch.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> This method is <b>not thread-safe</b>. Concurrent calls to mutation\n     * methods or reads during mutation will produce undefined results.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>CRC Impact:</b> This operation does <b>not</b> require CRC recomputation because the\n     * partition leader epoch field is intentionally excluded from the CRC. This allows brokers to\n     * update the epoch in-place for received batches without paying the cost of CRC recomputation.</p>\n     *\n     * @param epoch The new partition leader epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH}\n     *              if unknown\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int epoch) {\n        buffer.putInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long checksum() {\n        return ByteUtils.readUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validate that the CRC-32C checksum is correct.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance:</b> This method recomputes the CRC over all bytes from the attributes\n     * field to the end of the batch, then compares with the stored value. This is O(n) in the\n     * size of the batch and should be called judiciously.</p>\n     *\n     * @return {@code true} if the batch size is valid and CRC matches, {@code false} otherwise\n     */\n    public boolean isValid() {\n        return sizeInBytes() >= RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD && checksum() == computeChecksum();\n    }\n\n    private long computeChecksum() {\n        return Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, buffer.limit() - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private byte attributes() {\n        // note we're not using the second byte of attributes\n        return (byte) buffer.getShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        DefaultRecordBatch that = (DefaultRecordBatch) o;\n        return Objects.equals(buffer, that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer != null ? buffer.hashCode() : 0;\n    }\n\n    private static byte computeAttributes(CompressionType type, TimestampType timestampType,\n                                          boolean isTransactional, boolean isControl, boolean isDeleteHorizonSet) {\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timestamp type must be provided to compute attributes for message \" +\n                    \"format v2 and above\");\n\n        byte attributes = isTransactional ? TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK : 0;\n        if (isControl)\n            attributes |= CONTROL_FLAG_MASK;\n        if (type.id > 0)\n            attributes |= (byte) (COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK & type.id);\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            attributes |= TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK;\n        if (isDeleteHorizonSet)\n            attributes |= DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK;\n        return attributes;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write an empty batch header to the given buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>An empty batch (containing zero records) may still be retained after compaction to\n     * preserve producer sequence information for duplicate detection. This static helper\n     * initializes the complete batch header with specified metadata.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}; caller must ensure sufficient capacity\n     * @param magic The magic version (should be {@link RecordBatch#CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE})\n     * @param producerId The producer ID, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_ID}\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH}\n     * @param baseSequence The base sequence number, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_SEQUENCE}\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset of the batch\n     * @param lastOffset The last offset of the batch (same as base for single record)\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp value (creation time or log append time)\n     * @param isTransactional Whether this is a transactional batch\n     * @param isControlRecord Whether this is a control batch\n     */\n    public static void writeEmptyHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                        byte magic,\n                                        long producerId,\n                                        short producerEpoch,\n                                        int baseSequence,\n                                        long baseOffset,\n                                        long lastOffset,\n                                        int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                        TimestampType timestampType,\n                                        long timestamp,\n                                        boolean isTransactional,\n                                        boolean isControlRecord) {\n        int offsetDelta = (int) (lastOffset - baseOffset);\n        writeHeader(buffer, baseOffset, offsetDelta, DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD, magic,\n                    CompressionType.NONE, timestampType, RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP, timestamp, producerId,\n                    producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlRecord, false, partitionLeaderEpoch, 0);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write a complete batch header with all metadata fields.\n     *\n     * <p><b>CRC Computation:</b> This method automatically computes the CRC-32C over the\n     * attributes field through the end of the batch and writes it to the CRC field. The CRC\n     * covers all variable data (records), so callers must ensure the buffer position is\n     * correct relative to the batch structure.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Validation:</b> This method validates that the magic version is current; use of\n     * legacy magic versions will raise an exception.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param baseOffset The first offset in this batch\n     * @param lastOffsetDelta The delta from base offset to last offset\n     * @param sizeInBytes The total size of the batch including overhead\n     * @param magic The magic version (must be {@link RecordBatch#CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE})\n     * @param compressionType The {@link CompressionType}\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param baseTimestamp The timestamp of the first record (or NO_TIMESTAMP)\n     * @param maxTimestamp The maximum timestamp in the batch\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param epoch The producer epoch\n     * @param sequence The base sequence number\n     * @param isTransactional Whether this is a transactional batch\n     * @param isControlBatch Whether this is a control batch\n     * @param isDeleteHorizonSet Whether the delete horizon flag is set\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param numRecords The count of records in this batch\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException If magic version is not current or timestamp is invalid\n     */\n    public static void writeHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                   long baseOffset,\n                                   int lastOffsetDelta,\n                                   int sizeInBytes,\n                                   byte magic,\n                                   CompressionType compressionType,\n                                   TimestampType timestampType,\n                                   long baseTimestamp,\n                                   long maxTimestamp,\n                                   long producerId,\n                                   short epoch,\n                                   int sequence,\n                                   boolean isTransactional,\n                                   boolean isControlBatch,\n                                   boolean isDeleteHorizonSet,\n                                   int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                   int numRecords) {\n        if (magic < RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid magic value \" + magic);\n        if (baseTimestamp < 0 && baseTimestamp != NO_TIMESTAMP)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid message timestamp \" + baseTimestamp);\n\n        short attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType, timestampType, isTransactional, isControlBatch, isDeleteHorizonSet);\n\n        int position = buffer.position();\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, baseOffset);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LENGTH_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - LOG_OVERHEAD);\n        buffer.putInt(position + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n        buffer.put(position + MAGIC_OFFSET, magic);\n        buffer.putShort(position + ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, baseTimestamp);\n        buffer.putLong(position + MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET, lastOffsetDelta);\n        buffer.putLong(position + PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET, producerId);\n        buffer.putShort(position + PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n        buffer.putInt(position + BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET, sequence);\n        buffer.putInt(position + RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET, numRecords);\n        long crc = Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n        buffer.putInt(position + CRC_OFFSET, (int) crc);\n        buffer.position(position + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"RecordBatch(magic=\" + magic() + \", offsets=[\" + baseOffset() + \", \" + lastOffset() + \"], \" +\n                \"sequence=[\" + baseSequence() + \", \" + lastSequence() + \"], \" +\n                \"partitionLeaderEpoch=\" + partitionLeaderEpoch() + \", \" +\n                \"isTransactional=\" + isTransactional() + \", isControlBatch=\" + isControlBatch() + \", \" +\n                \"compression=\" + compressionType() + \", timestampType=\" + timestampType() + \", crc=\" + checksum() + \")\";\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Estimate the total size needed for a batch containing the given records.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Note:</b> This is an inclusive estimation that accounts for the batch overhead\n     * and all record serialization. The estimate is precise for uncompressed batches but may\n     * be less accurate for compressed batches since compression ratios are not known in advance.</p>\n     *\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset of the batch\n     * @param records An iterable of {@link Record}s to be included\n     * @return The estimated size in bytes including batch overhead\n     */\n    public static int sizeInBytes(long baseOffset, Iterable<Record> records) {\n        Iterator<Record> iterator = records.iterator();\n        if (!iterator.hasNext())\n            return 0;\n\n        int size = RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD;\n        Long baseTimestamp = null;\n        while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n            Record record = iterator.next();\n            int offsetDelta = (int) (record.offset() - baseOffset);\n            if (baseTimestamp == null)\n                baseTimestamp = record.timestamp();\n            long timestampDelta = record.timestamp() - baseTimestamp;\n            size += DefaultRecord.sizeInBytes(offsetDelta, timestampDelta, record.key(), record.value(),\n                    record.headers());\n        }\n        return size;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Estimate the total size needed for a batch containing the given simple records.\n     *\n     * @param records An iterable of {@link SimpleRecord}s to be included\n     * @return The estimated size in bytes including batch overhead\n     */\n    public static int sizeInBytes(Iterable<SimpleRecord> records) {\n        Iterator<SimpleRecord> iterator = records.iterator();\n        if (!iterator.hasNext())\n            return 0;\n\n        int size = RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD;\n        int offsetDelta = 0;\n        Long baseTimestamp = null;\n        while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n            SimpleRecord record = iterator.next();\n            if (baseTimestamp == null)\n                baseTimestamp = record.timestamp();\n            long timestampDelta = record.timestamp() - baseTimestamp;\n            size += DefaultRecord.sizeInBytes(offsetDelta++, timestampDelta, record.key(), record.value(),\n                    record.headers());\n        }\n        return size;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get an upper bound on the size of a batch with only a single record.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Note:</b> This is a conservative estimate that does not account for compression\n     * algorithms' potential to reduce the final size.</p>\n     *\n     * @param key The key byte buffer, or null\n     * @param value The value byte buffer, or null\n     * @param headers The headers array, or null\n     * @return An upper bound on the batch size in bytes\n     */\n    static int estimateBatchSizeUpperBound(ByteBuffer key, ByteBuffer value, Header[] headers) {\n        return RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + DefaultRecord.recordSizeUpperBound(key, value, headers);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Increment a sequence number by the given amount, handling wrap-around at {@link Integer#MAX_VALUE}.\n     *\n     * <p>Sequence numbers in Kafka wrap around at {@code Integer.MAX_VALUE}, so this method\n     * correctly handles the wrap-around case.</p>\n     *\n     * @param sequence The base sequence number\n     * @param increment The amount to increment by\n     * @return The incremented sequence number, handling wrap-around\n     */\n    public static int incrementSequence(int sequence, int increment) {\n        if (sequence > Integer.MAX_VALUE - increment)\n            return increment - (Integer.MAX_VALUE - sequence) - 1;\n        return sequence + increment;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Decrement a sequence number by the given amount, handling wrap-around.\n     *\n     * @param sequence The base sequence number\n     * @param decrement The amount to decrement by\n     * @return The decremented sequence number, handling wrap-around\n     */\n    public static int decrementSequence(int sequence, int decrement) {\n        if (sequence < decrement)\n            return Integer.MAX_VALUE - (decrement - sequence) + 1;\n        return sequence - decrement;\n    }\n\n    // visible for testing\n    abstract class RecordIterator implements CloseableIterator<Record> {\n        private final Long logAppendTime;\n        private final long baseOffset;\n        private final long baseTimestamp;\n        private final int baseSequence;\n        private final int numRecords;\n        private int readRecords = 0;\n\n        RecordIterator() {\n            this.logAppendTime = timestampType() == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ? maxTimestamp() : null;\n            this.baseOffset = baseOffset();\n            this.baseTimestamp = baseTimestamp();\n            this.baseSequence = baseSequence();\n            int numRecords = count();\n            if (numRecords < 0)\n                throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Found invalid record count \" + numRecords + \" in magic v\" +\n                        magic() + \" batch\");\n            this.numRecords = numRecords;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public boolean hasNext() {\n            return readRecords < numRecords;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public Record next() {\n            if (readRecords >= numRecords)\n                throw new NoSuchElementException();\n\n            readRecords++;\n            Record rec = readNext(baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n            if (readRecords == numRecords) {\n                // Validate that the actual size of the batch is equal to declared size\n                // by checking that after reading declared number of items, there no items left\n                // (overflow case, i.e. reading past buffer end is checked elsewhere).\n                if (!ensureNoneRemaining())\n                    throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Incorrect declared batch size, records still remaining in file\");\n            }\n            return rec;\n        }\n\n        protected abstract Record readNext(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime);\n\n        protected abstract boolean ensureNoneRemaining();\n\n        @Override\n        public void remove() {\n            throw new UnsupportedOperationException();\n        }\n\n    }\n\n    // visible for testing\n    abstract class StreamRecordIterator extends RecordIterator {\n        private final InputStream inputStream;\n\n        StreamRecordIterator(InputStream inputStream) {\n            super();\n            this.inputStream = inputStream;\n        }\n\n        abstract Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException;\n\n        @Override\n        protected Record readNext(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) {\n            try {\n                return doReadRecord(baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n            } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {\n                throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Incorrect declared batch size, premature EOF reached\", e);\n            } catch (IOException e) {\n                throw new KafkaException(\"Failed to decompress record stream\", e);\n            }\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        protected boolean ensureNoneRemaining() {\n            try {\n                return inputStream.read() == -1;\n            } catch (IOException e) {\n                throw new KafkaException(\"Error checking for remaining bytes after reading batch\", e);\n            }\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void close() {\n            try {\n                inputStream.close();\n            } catch (IOException e) {\n                throw new KafkaException(\"Failed to close record stream\", e);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    static class DefaultFileChannelRecordBatch extends FileLogInputStream.FileChannelRecordBatch {\n\n        DefaultFileChannelRecordBatch(long offset,\n                                      byte magic,\n                                      FileRecords fileRecords,\n                                      int position,\n                                      int batchSize) {\n            super(offset, magic, fileRecords, position, batchSize);\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        protected RecordBatch toMemoryRecordBatch(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n            return new DefaultRecordBatch(buffer);\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public long baseOffset() {\n            return offset;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public long lastOffset() {\n            return loadBatchHeader().lastOffset();\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public long producerId() {\n            return Callers must ensure external synchronization\n * or create separate instances if multiple threads need concurrent access. However, since batches are\n * typically read-only after creation, sharing immutable batch instances across threads is safe.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Binary Format:</b> The v2 record batch consists of a fixed header (56 bytes) followed by\n * variable-length record data. The CRC covers all bytes after the magic byte, including attributes,\n * timestamps, producer IDs, sequence numbers, and record data. The partition leader epoch is\n * intentionally excluded from the CRC to allow brokers to update it in-place without recomputation.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Schema:</b>\n * <pre>{@code\n *   RecordBatch =>\n *     BaseOffset => Int64\n *     Length => Int32\n *     PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\n *     Magic => Int8\n *     CRC => Uint32\n *     Attributes => Int16\n *     LastOffsetDelta => Int32\n *     BaseTimestamp => Int64\n *     MaxTimestamp => Int64\n *     ProducerId => Int64\n *     ProducerEpoch => Int16\n *     BaseSequence => Int32\n *     RecordsCount => Int32\n *     Records => [Record]\n * }</pre>\n * </p>\n *\n * <p><b>Compression:</b> When compression is enabled, the compressed record data immediately\n * follows the record count field. Decompression is handled transparently by {@link #streamingIterator}\n * and related methods.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Compaction Behavior:</b> During log compaction, the base and last offsets/sequences are\n * preserved from the original batch to maintain producer state integrity. This ensures that after\n * a broker restart, the producer's expected next sequence number remains in sync with the broker's\n * state, preventing spurious OutOfOrderSequence errors.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Attributes:</b> The 16-bit attributes field encodes compression type, timestamp type,\n * transactional flag, control flag, and delete horizon flag. The upper 10 bits are currently unused\n * and must be zero for forward compatibility.</p>\n *\n * @see RecordBatch\n * @see MutableRecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecords\n */\npublic class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch implements MutableRecordBatch {\n    // Field offset constants for binary format layout\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET = 0;\n    static final = LENGTH_OFFSET + LENGTH_LENGTH;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int MAGIC_OFFSET = PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAGIC_LENGTH = 1;\n    public static final int CRC_OFFSET = MAGIC_OFFSET + MAGIC_LENGTH;\n    static final int CRC_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET = CRC_OFFSET + CRC_LENGTH;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH = 2;\n    public static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET = ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET + ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH;\n    static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET = PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH = 4;\n    public static final int RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET = BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET + BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH;\n    static final int RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int RECORDS_OFFSET = RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET + RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH;\n    public static final int RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD = RECORDS_OFFSET;\n\n    // Attribute bit masks\n    private static final byte COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK = 0x07;\n    private static final byte TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK = 0x10;\n    private static final int CONTROL_FLAG_MASK = 0x20;\n    private static final byte DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK = 0x40;\n    private static final byte TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK = 0x08;\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    /**\n     * Construct a {@code DefaultRecordBatch} wrapping the given buffer.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> The caller is responsible for ensuring that the buffer\n     * is not modified concurrently while this batch is in use.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer A {@link ByteBuffer} positioned at the start of a magic v2 batch.\n     *               The buffer must contain at least {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes\n     *               and remain valid for the lifetime of this batch instance.\n     */\n    DefaultRecordBatch(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public byte magic() {\n        return buffer.get(MAGIC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void ensureValid() {\n        if (sizeInBytes() < RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD)\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record batch is corrupt (the size \" + sizeInBytes() +\n                    \" is smaller than the minimum allowed overhead \" + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + \")\");\n\n        if (!isValid())\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record is corrupt (stored crc = \" + checksum()\n                    + \", computed crc = \" + computeChecksum() + \")\");\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Gets the base timestamp of the batch, which is used to calculate individual record timestamps\n     * by adding per-record timestamp deltas.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Semantics:</b>\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>If the batch is not empty: timestamp of the first record in the original batch</li>\n     *   <li>If the batch is empty: set to {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} (which is -1)</li>\n     *   <li>If delete horizon is set: the delete horizon timestamp (used during compaction)</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return The base timestamp in milliseconds since epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP}\n     *         if empty or not applicable\n     */\n    public long baseTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long maxTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TimestampType timestampType() {\n        return (attributes() & TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK) == 0 ? TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long baseOffset() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long lastOffset() {\n        return baseOffset() + lastOffsetDelta();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long producerId() {\n        return buffer.getLong(PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public short producerEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getShort(PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int baseSequence() {\n        return buffer.getInt(BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int lastOffsetDelta() {\n        return buffer.getInt(LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int lastSequence() {\n        int baseSequence = baseSequence();\n        if (baseSequence == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n            return RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE;\n        return incrementSequence(baseSequence, lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CompressionType compressionType() {\n        return CompressionType.forId(attributes() & COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return LOG_OVERHEAD + buffer.getInt(LENGTH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int count() {\n        return buffer.getInt(RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Integer countOrNull() {\n        return count();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch to the given buffer without decompression.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance:</b> This is a zero-copy operation that uses a buffer duplicate.\n     * If the batch is compressed, the compressed data is written as-is.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}; must have at least\n     *               {@link #sizeInBytes()} remaining bytes\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        buffer.put(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch to the given stream.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance:</b> This operation may be more efficient than {@link #writeTo(ByteBuffer)}\n     * for certain {@link ByteBufferOutputStream} implementations that support bulk writes.</p>\n     *\n     * @param outputStream The destination {@link ByteBufferOutputStream}; must have capacity\n     *                     for at least {@link #sizeInBytes()} bytes\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBufferOutputStream outputStream) {\n        outputStream.write(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isTransactional() {\n        return (attributes() & TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    private boolean hasDeleteHorizonMs() {\n        return (attributes() & DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs() {\n        if (hasDeleteHorizonMs())\n            return OptionalLong.of(buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET));\n        else\n            return OptionalLong.empty();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isControlBatch() {\n        return (attributes() & CONTROL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int partitionLeaderEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create an input stream for reading the serialized record data of this batch.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Compression Handling:</b> If the batch is compressed, the returned stream\n     * automatically decompresses data as it is read. The decompression is performed using\n     * the compression type specified in the batch attributes and the provided buffer supplier.</p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier of {@link ByteBuffer}s for decompression buffers.\n     *                       For optimal performance, the supplier should reuse buffers across calls.\n     * @return An {@link InputStream} positioned at the start of the records section.\n     *         For compressed batches, the stream wraps a decompression wrapper.\n     */\n    public InputStream recordInputStream(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return Compression.of(compressionType()).build().wrapForInput(buffer, magic(), bufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> compressedIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier, boolean skipKeyValue) {\n        final InputStream inputStream = recordInputStream(bufferSupplier);\n\n        if (skipKeyValue) {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readPartiallyFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        } else {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        }\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> uncompressedIterator() {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return new RecordIterator() {\n            @Override\n            protected Record readNext(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) {\n                try {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(buffer, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                } catch (BufferUnderflowException e) {\n                    throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Incorrect declared batch size, premature EOF reached\");\n                }\n            }\n            @Override\n            protected boolean ensureNoneRemaining() {\n                return !buffer.hasRemaining();\n            }\n            @Override\n            public void close() {}\n        };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return an iterator over records in this batch, decompressing if necessary.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Compression Handling:</b> If the batch is compressed, this method fully decompresses\n     * the record stream into memory before returning an iterator. This approach trades memory for\n     * simplicity and resource safety (the returned iterator does not need to be closed).\n     * For memory-constrained scenarios, prefer {@link #streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)}.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Empty Batches:</b> If the batch contains no records, returns an empty iterator.</p>\n     *\n     * @return An {@link Iterator} over {@link Record}s; safe to use in enhanced for-loops\n     *         and does not require explicit closure\n     */\n    @Override\n    public Iterator<Record> iterator() {\n        if (count() == 0)\n            return Collections.emptyIterator();\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // for a normal iterator, we cannot ensure that the underlying compression stream is closed,\n        // so we decompress the full record set here. Use cases which call for a lower memory footprint\n        // can use `streamingIterator` at the cost of additional complexity\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = compressedIterator(BufferSupplier.NO_CACHING, false)) {\n            List<Record> records = new ArrayList<>(count());\n            while (iterator.hasNext())\n                records.add(iterator.next());\n            return records.iterator();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a closeable iterator that skips over record key/value/header data during iteration.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Use Case:</b> This is useful for operations that only need record metadata (offsets,\n     * timestamps, producer IDs) without the actual record content. This can significantly reduce\n     * memory usage and improve performance compared to fully reading every record.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance Note:</b>\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>For compressed batches: Uses a streaming decompression iterator with skipping enabled</li>\n     *   <li>For uncompressed batches: Falls back to normal iteration since skipping is less efficient\n     *       than just reading through the data</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier for decompression buffers if the batch is compressed\n     * @return A {@link CloseableIterator} over records with minimal data loading;\n     *         must be closed by the caller if the batch is compressed\n     */\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> skipKeyValueIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (count() == 0) {\n            return CloseableIterator.wrap(Collections.emptyIterator());\n        }\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // we define this to be a closable iterator so that caller (i.e. the log validator) needs to close it\n        // while we can save memory footprint of not decompressing the full record set ahead of time\n        return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, true);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return a streaming iterator for lazy decompression and record parsing.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Memory Efficiency:</b> For compressed batches, this iterator decompresses data\n     * on-demand as {@link Iterator#next()} is called, rather than loading the entire decompressed\n     * stream into memory. This is critical for memory-constrained scenarios or when processing\n     * large batches.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Resource Management:</b> The returned iterator must be explicitly closed\n     * (preferably via try-with-resources) to release decompression resources.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Buffer Supplier Recommendation:</b> Provide a {@link BufferSupplier} that\n     * reuses buffers across multiple iterations. This significantly improves performance\n     * by avoiding repeated allocations of large decompression buffers (e.g., 64 KB for LZ4).</p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier for decompression buffers. Suppliers that reuse\n     *                       buffers across calls have significant performance impact.\n     * @return A {@link CloseableIterator} that enables lazy decompression; must be closed by caller\n     */\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (isCompressed())\n            return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, false);\n        else\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Modify the last offset of this batch (as a mutable batch).\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> This method is <b>not thread-safe</b>. Concurrent calls to mutation\n     * methods or reads during mutation will produce undefined results.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>CRC Impact:</b> This method updates only the base offset to maintain the correct\n     * offset delta. The CRC remains valid since the offset fields are outside the CRC computation.</p>\n     *\n     * @param offset The new last offset for this batch; the base offset is automatically\n     *               adjusted to maintain the offset delta\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void setLastOffset(long offset) {\n        buffer.putLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, offset - lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Modify the maximum timestamp and timestamp type of this batch.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> This method is <b>not thread-safe</b>. Concurrent calls to mutation\n     * methods or reads during mutation will produce undefined results.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>CRC Recomputation:</b> If the timestamp or timestamp type changes, the CRC is\n     * automatically recomputed since both fields are covered by the checksum.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Optimization:</b> If the new values match the current ones, no modification occurs\n     * and CRC recomputation is skipped.</p>\n     *\n     * @param timestampType The new {@link TimestampType} for this batch\n     * @param maxTimestamp The new maximum timestamp in milliseconds since epoch\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType timestampType, long maxTimestamp) {\n        long currentMaxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        // We don't need to recompute crc if the timestamp is not updated.\n        if (timestampType() == timestampType && currentMaxTimestamp == maxTimestamp)\n            return;\n\n        byte attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType(), timestampType, isTransactional(), isControlBatch(), hasDeleteHorizonMs());\n        buffer.putShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        long crc = computeChecksum();\n        ByteUtils.writeUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET, crc);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set the partition leader epoch for this batch.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> This method is <b>not thread-safe</b>. Concurrent calls to mutation\n     * methods or reads during mutation will produce undefined results.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>CRC Impact:</b> This operation does <b>not</b> require CRC recomputation because the\n     * partition leader epoch field is intentionally excluded from the CRC. This allows brokers to\n     * update the epoch in-place for received batches without paying the cost of CRC recomputation.</p>\n     *\n     * @param epoch The new partition leader epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH}\n     *              if unknown\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int epoch) {\n        buffer.putInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long checksum() {\n        return ByteUtils.readUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validate that the CRC-32C checksum is correct.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance:</b> This method recomputes the CRC over all bytes from the attributes\n     * field to the end of the batch, then compares with the stored value. This is O(n) in the\n     * size of the batch and should be called judiciously.</p>\n     *\n     * @return {@code true} if the batch size is valid and CRC matches, {@code false} otherwise\n     */\n    public boolean isValid() {\n        return sizeInBytes() >= RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD && checksum() == computeChecksum();\n    }\n\n    private long computeChecksum() {\n        return Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, buffer.limit() - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private byte attributes() {\n        // note we're not using the second byte of attributes\n        return (byte) buffer.getShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        DefaultRecordBatch that = (DefaultRecordBatch) o;\n        return Objects.equals(buffer, that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer != null ? buffer.hashCode() : 0;\n    }\n\n    private static byte computeAttributes(CompressionType type, TimestampType timestampType,\n                                          boolean isTransactional, boolean isControl, boolean isDeleteHorizonSet) {\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timestamp type must be provided to compute attributes for message \" +\n                    \"format v2 and above\");\n\n        byte attributes = isTransactional ? TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK : 0;\n        if (isControl)\n            attributes |= CONTROL_FLAG_MASK;\n        if (type.id > 0)\n            attributes |= (byte) (COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK & type.id);\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            attributes |= TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK;\n        if (isDeleteHorizonSet)\n            attributes |= DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK;\n        return attributes;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write an empty batch header to the given buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>An empty batch (containing zero records) may still be retained after compaction to\n     * preserve producer sequence information for duplicate detection. This static helper\n     * initializes the complete batch header with specified metadata.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}; caller must ensure sufficient capacity\n     * @param magic The magic version (should be {@link RecordBatch#CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE})\n     * @param producerId The producer ID, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_ID}\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH}\n     * @param baseSequence The base sequence number, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_SEQUENCE}\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset of the batch\n     * @param lastOffset The last offset of the batch (same as base for single record)\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp value (creation time or log append time)\n     * @param isTransactional Whether this is a transactional batch\n     * @param isControlRecord Whether this is a control batch\n     */\n    public static void writeEmptyHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                        byte magic,\n                                        long producerId,\n                                        short producerEpoch,\n                                        int baseSequence,\n                                        long baseOffset,\n                                        long lastOffset,\n                                        int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                        TimestampType timestampType,\n                                        long timestamp,\n                                        boolean isTransactional,\n                                        boolean isControlRecord) {\n        int offsetDelta = (int) (lastOffset - baseOffset);\n        writeHeader(buffer, baseOffset, offsetDelta, DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD, magic,\n                    CompressionType.NONE, timestampType, RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP, timestamp, producerId,\n                    producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlRecord, false, partitionLeaderEpoch, 0);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write a complete batch header with all metadata fields.\n     *\n     * <p><b>CRC Computation:</b> This method automatically computes the CRC-32C over the\n     * attributes field through the end of the batch and writes it to the CRC field. The CRC\n     * covers all variable data (records), so callers must ensure the buffer position is\n     * correct relative to the batch structure.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Validation:</b> This method This is typically used for:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Reading incoming produce requests from clients</li>\n *   <li>Reading log segments from disk (after loading into memory)</li>\n *   <li>Filtering records during log compaction</li>\n *   <li>Validating record batches for correctness</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n *\n * <p><b>Construction:</b> To create a new buffer of record batches, use {@link #builder(ByteBuffer, byte, Compression, TimestampType, long)}\n * or one of its variants. For reading existing data, use {@link #readableRecords(ByteBuffer)}.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Thread Safety:</b> {@code MemoryRecords} instances are <b>not thread-safe</b> for concurrent\n * modification, but the underlying buffer is typically immutable after construction. Multiple threads\n * may safely read from the same instance concurrently if the buffer contents are not being modified.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Memory Efficiency:</b> The buffer is stored as-is without copying. The {@link #buffer()} method\n * returns a duplicate to prevent unintended position changes from affecting batch iteration.</p>\n *\n * <p><b>Lazy Evaluation:</b> Batch iteration is lazy; batches are parsed on-demand as you iterate.\n * Validation (via {@link RecordBatch#isValid()}) is not automatic and must be explicitly requested.</p>\n *\n * @see RecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder\n * @see Records\n */\npublic class MemoryRecords extends AbstractRecords {\n    /**\n     * An empty {@code MemoryRecords} instance, useful as a sentinel or default value.\n     */\n    public static final MemoryRecords EMPTY = MemoryRecords.readableRecords(ByteBuffer.allocate(0));\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    private final Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches = this::batchIterator;\n\n    private int validBytes = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Construct a {@code MemoryRecords} backed by the given buffer.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Ownership:</b> The caller retains ownership of the buffer. *               Must not be null.\n     * @throws NullPointerException if buffer is null\n     */\n    private MemoryRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        Objects.requireNonNull(buffer, \"buffer should not be null\");\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return buffer.limit();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write a portion of these records to the given channel.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Partial Writes:</b> This method supports writing a subset of the records buffer.\n     * The {@code position} and {@code length} parameters define the slice to be written.</p>\n     *\n     * @param channel The {@link TransferableChannel} to write to\n     * @param position The starting position within this buffer (0-based)\n     * @param length The buffer limit\n     */\n    @Override\n    public int writeTo(TransferableChannel channel, int position, int length) throws IOException {\n        if (((long) position) + length > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"position+length should not be greater than buffer.limit(), position: \"\n                    + position + \", length: \" + length + \", buffer.limit(): \" + buffer.limit());\n\n        return Utils.tryWriteTo(channel, position, length, buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write all records to the given channel, including any partial trailing records.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Completeness:</b> Unlike {@link #writeTo(TransferableChannel, int, int)},\n     * this method writes the entire buffer including potentially incomplete batches at the end.</p>\n     *\n     * @param channel The {@link GatheringByteChannel} to write to\n     * @return The total number of bytes written\n     * @throws IOException For any I/O errors writing to the channel\n     */\n    public int writeFullyTo(GatheringByteChannel channel) throws IOException {\n        buffer.mark();\n        int written = 0;\n        while (written < sizeInBytes())\n            written += channel.write(buffer);\n        buffer.reset();\n        return written;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get the total number of bytes in this record set representing valid, complete record batches.\n included.\n     * This may be smaller than {@link #sizeInBytes()}.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Caching:</b> This value is computed once and then cached on first access.\n     * If batches are modified in-place, the cache becomes stale.</p>\n     *\n     * @return The number of valid bytes, excluding any trailing partial batches\n     */\n    public int validBytes() {\n        if (validBytes >= 0)\n            return validBytes;\n\n        int bytes = 0;\n        for (RecordBatch batch : batches())\n            bytes += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n        this.validBytes = bytes;\n        return bytes;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public AbstractIterator<MutableRecordBatch> batchIterator() {\n        return new RecordBatchIterator<>(new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer.duplicate(), Records may be selectively retained or discarded based on the filter.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Output Buffer Management:</b> If the filtered output does not fit in the provided\n     * {@code destinationBuffer}, a new buffer is allocated and returned in the {@link FilterResult}.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Compaction Support:</b> If filtered records contain tombstones or aborted transaction markers,\n     * the delete horizon is automatically set to enable proper tombstone cleanup during future compaction.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance Tuning:</b> The {@code decompressionBufferSupplier} is critical for performance.\n     * A supplier that reuses buffers across calls significantly improves throughput, especially for\n     * LZ4 compression which requires 64 KB buffers.</p>\n     *\n     * @param filter The {@link RecordFilter} that determines retention policy\n     * @param destinationBuffer The {@link ByteBuffer} to write filtered records to;\n     *                          may be replaced in the result if insufficient capacity\n     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier A supplier for decompression buffers. *         and metadata for metrics\n     * @see RecordFilter\n     * @see FilterResult\n     */\n    public FilterResult filterTo(RecordFilter filter, ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier
