first timestamp of the batch (which is usually the timestamp of the first record)\n     * to the delete horizon of the tombstones or txn markers which are present in the batch.\n     */\n    private static FilterResult filterTo(Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches, RecordFilter filter,\n                                         ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        FilterResult filterResult = new FilterResult(destinationBuffer);\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(destinationBuffer);\n        for (MutableRecordBatch batch : batches) {\n            final BatchRetentionResult batchRetentionResult = filter.checkBatchRetention(batch);\n            final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = batchRetentionResult.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            final BatchRetention batchRetention = batchRetentionResult.batchRetention;\n\n            filterResult.bytesRead += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n            if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.DELETE)\n                continue;\n\n            final BatchFilterResult iterationResult = filterBatch(batch, decompressionBufferSupplier, filterResult,\n                filter);\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = iterationResult.retainedRecords;\n            boolean containsTombstones = iterationResult.containsTombstones;\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = iterationResult.writeOriginalBatch;\n            long maxOffset = iterationResult.maxOffset;\n\n            if (!retainedRecords.isEmpty()) {\n                // we check if the delete horizon should be set to a new value\n                // in which case, we need to reset the base timestamp and overwrite the timestamp deltas\n                // if the batch does not contain tombstones, then we don't need to overwrite batch\n                boolean needToSetDeleteHorizon = (containsTombstones || containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) &&\n                    batch.deleteHorizonMs().isEmpty();\n                if (writeOriginalBatch && !needToSetDeleteHorizon) {\n                    batch.writeTo(bufferOutputStream);\n                    filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, retainedRecords.size(), false);\n                } else {\n                    long deleteHorizonMs;\n                    if (needToSetDeleteHorizon)\n                        deleteHorizonMs = filter.currentTime + filter.deleteRetentionMs;\n                    else\n                        deleteHorizonMs = batch.deleteHorizonMs().orElse(RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP);\n                    try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = buildRetainedRecordsInto(batch, retainedRecords,\n                            bufferOutputStream, deleteHorizonMs)) {\n                        MemoryRecords records = builder.build();\n                        int filteredBatchSize = records.sizeInBytes();\n                        MemoryRecordsBuilder.RecordsInfo info = builder.info();\n                        filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(info.maxTimestamp, info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\n                            maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\n                if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\");\n\n                bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n                DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\n                        batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\n                        batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\n                        batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\n                filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\n            }\n\n            // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\n            // avoid the need for additional allocations.\n            ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\n            if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\n                filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n                return filterResult;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return filterResult;\n    }\n\n    private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n            long maxOffset = -1;\n            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n            // Convert records with old record versions\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iterator.next();\n                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n\n                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n\n                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n\n                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n                        containsTombstones = true;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n                }\n            }\n            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n                                  final long maxOffset) {\n            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n\n        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n\n        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n            builder.append(record);\n\n        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n\n        return builder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get a duplicate of the byte buffer that backs this instance.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Position Independence:</b> Returning a duplicate ensures that position/limit\n     * changes made by callers do not affect the internal buffer position.</p>\n     *\n     * @return A {@link ByteBuffer} duplicate containing this record set\n     */\n    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n        return buffer.duplicate();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@code MemoryRecords} view containing a slice of this buffer.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Zero-Copy:</b> The returned instance shares the underlying buffer; no data is copied.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Boundary Conditions:</b> The slice may start or end in the middle of a record batch.\n     * Callers must be aware that {@link #validBytes()} may differ from the slice size.</p>\n     *\n     * @param position The starting position in this buffer (0-based, inclusive)\n     * @param size The number of bytes to include in the slice\n     * @return A new {@code MemoryRecords} instance backed by the sliced buffer\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException If position or size are invalid\n     */\n    @Override\n    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n        if (position < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n        if (position > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n        if (size < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n\n        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n\n        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n        return batches;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n                \")\";\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n\n        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer.hashCode();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Abstract base class for filtering record batches and individual records during log compaction.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Filtering Levels:</b>\n     * <ol>\n     *   <li>{@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)} — decides if an entire batch should be deleted\n     *       without examining records. This is useful for optimizing deletion of large batches.</li>\n     *   <li>{@link #shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch, Record)} — decides if individual records\n     *       should be retained (e.g., based on TTL, topic configuration, or record key).</li>\n     * </ol>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Compaction Semantics:</b> The filter is called during log compaction to:\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>Discard stale records (those with earlier versions of the same key)</li>\n     *   <li>Enforce retention policies (delete records older than a TTL)</li>\n     *   <li>Clean up tombstones and transaction markers</li>\n     *   <li>Up-convert old message formats to the current version</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @see FilterResult\n     */\n    public abstract static class RecordFilter {\n        /** The current time used for TTL calculations, in milliseconds since epoch. */\n        public final long currentTime;\n        /** The number of milliseconds to retain tombstones and transaction markers. */\n        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n\n        /**\n         * Construct a filter with the given time parameters.\n         *\n         * @param currentTime The current time in milliseconds since epoch\n         * @param deleteRetentionMs The minimum duration to retain deletion markers\n         */\n        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Result of batch-level retention check.\n         */\n        public static class BatchRetentionResult {\n            /** The batch retention decision. */\n            public final BatchRetention batchRetention;\n            /** Whether this batch contains an end-of-transaction marker for an empty transaction. */\n            public final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n\n            /**\n             * Construct a batch retention result.\n             *\n             * @param batchRetention The retention decision\n             * @param containsMarkerForEmptyTxn Whether the batch contains an empty transaction marker\n             */\n            public BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Decision enum for batch-level retention.\n         */\n        public enum BatchRetention {\n            /** Delete the batch entirely without inspecting records. */\n            DELETE,\n            /** Retain the batch even if it is empty. */\n            RETAIN_EMPTY,\n            /** Delete the batch only if it becomes empty after filtering. */\n            DELETE_EMPTY\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether the full batch can be discarded without inspecting individual records.\n         *\n         * <p><b>Optimization:</b> This method is called first and avoids iteration overhead for\n         * batches that can be entirely discarded (e.g., all records are too old).</p>\n         *\n         * @param batch The {@link RecordBatch} to evaluate\n         * @return A {@link BatchRetentionResult} indicating the decision\n         */\n        protected abstract BatchRetentionResult checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch batch);\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether a record should be retained in the log.\n         *\n         * <p><b>Invocation:</b> This method is called only for records in batches that were not\n         * entirely discarded by {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}.</p>\n         *\n         * <p><b>Example Logic:</b> A real implementation might check:\n         * <ul>\n         *   <li>Record key uniqueness (keep only the latest version)</li>\n         *   <li>Record age (discard records older than the log retention period)</li>\n         *   <li>Tombstone retention (keep tombstones for a grace period to ensure eventual consistency)</li>\n         * </ul>\n         * </p>\n         *\n         * @param recordBatch The {@link RecordBatch} containing the record\n         * @param record The {@link Record} to evaluate\n         * @return {@code true} if the record should be kept, {@code false} if it should be discarded\n         */\n        protected abstract boolean shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch recordBatch, Record record);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Result of filtering a set of record batches.\n     *\n     * <p>This class summarizes the input/output metrics of the filtering operation,\n     * useful for logging and monitoring compaction progress.</p>\n     */\n    public static class FilterResult {\n        /** The output buffer containing filtered records. May be reallocated if insufficient capacity. */\n        private ByteBuffer outputBuffer;\n        /** Total number of records (messages) read during filtering. */\n        private int messagesRead = 0;\n        /** Total number of bytes read from input batches. */\n        private int bytesRead = 0;\n        /** Total number of records retained in the output. */\n        private int messagesRetained = 0;\n        /** Total number of bytes written to the output buffer. */\n        private int bytesRetained = 0;\n        /** The maximum offset of any retained record. */\n        private long maxOffset = -1L;\n        /** The maximum timestamp of any retained record. */\n        private long maxTimestamp = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        /** The offset of the record with the maximum timestamp (at a shallow level). */\n        private long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = -1L;\n\n        /**\n         * Construct a filter result with the given output buffer.\n         *\n         * @param outputBuffer The {@link ByteBuffer} to accumulate filtered records in\n         */\n        private FilterResult(ByteBuffer outputBuffer) {\n            this.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(MutableRecordBatch retainedBatch, int numMessagesInBatch, boolean headerOnly) {\n            int bytesRetained = headerOnly ? DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD : retainedBatch.sizeInBytes();\n            updateRetainedBatchMetadata(retainedBatch.maxTimestamp(), retainedBatch.lastOffset(),\n                    retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n            }\n            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        private void validateBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset) {\n            if (maxTimestamp != RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP && shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"shallowOffset undefined for maximum timestamp \" + maxTimestamp);\n            if (maxOffset < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"maxOffset undefined\");\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the output buffer containing filtered records.\n         *\n         * @return The {@link ByteBuffer} with filtered records\n         */\n        public ByteBuffer outputBuffer() {\n            return outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of records read during filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The count of input records examined\n         */\n        public int messagesRead() {\n            return messagesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of bytes read from input batches.\n         *\n         * @return The count of input bytes\n         */\n        public int bytesRead() {\n            return bytesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of records retained in the output.\n         *\n         * @return The count of output records\n         */\n        public int messagesRetained() {\n            return messagesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of bytes written to the output buffer.\n         *\n         * @return The count of output bytes\n         */\n        public int bytesRetained() {\n            return bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum offset of any retained record.\n         *\n         * @return The highest offset, or -1L if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long maxOffset() {\n            return maxOffset;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum timestamp of any retained record.\n         *\n         * @return The highest timestamp value\n         */\n        public long maxTimestamp() {\n            return maxTimestamp;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the offset of the record with the maximum timestamp.\n         *\n         * @return The offset at the maximum timestamp, or -1L if none\n         */\n        public long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n            return shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@code MemoryRecords} instance wrapping the given buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>This factory method is the standard way to create a read-only view of serialized record batches.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer A {@link ByteBuffer} containing one or more serialized record batches\n     * @return A {@code MemoryRecords} instance backed by the buffer\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords readableRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        return new MemoryRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a builder for writing records with default settings.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Defaults:</b>\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>Magic version: {@link RecordBatch#CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE}</li>\n     *   <li>Base offset: as provided</li>\n     *   <li>Producer ID: {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_ID}</li>\n     *   <li>Transactional: false</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm to use\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param baseOffset The starting offset for records in this batch\n     * @return A {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for appending records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a builder with a maximum batch size constraint.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param baseOffset The starting offset\n     * @param maxSize The maximum size in bytes for the output batch; builder may stop early if exceeded\n     * @return A {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for appending records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               int maxSize) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n            logAppendTime, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE,\n            false, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH, maxSize);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a builder with custom magic version and log append time.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param magic The record format version\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param baseOffset The starting offset\n     * @param logAppendTime The timestamp to use for {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}\n     * @return A {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for appending records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a builder with custom magic version and auto-generated log append time if needed.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param magic The record format version\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param baseOffset The starting offset\n     * @return A {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for appending records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a builder with partition leader epoch.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param magic The record format version\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param baseOffset The starting offset\n     * @param logAppendTime The log append time\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The current partition leader epoch\n     * @return A {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for appending records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a builder for idempotent records.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Idempotence:</b> Records are marked with a producer ID, epoch, and base sequence\n     * to enable exactly-once semantics.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param baseOffset The starting offset\n     * @param producerId The producer's ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer's epoch\n     * @param baseSequence The starting sequence number\n     * @param isTransactional Whether these records are part of a transaction\n     * @return A {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for appending     long baseOffset,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, baseOffset,\n                RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a builder with producer information.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param magic The record format version\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param baseOffset The starting offset\n     * @param logAppendTime The log append time\n     * @param producerId The producer's ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer's epoch\n     * @param baseSequence The starting sequence number\n     * @return A {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for appending records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a builder with full configuration.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param magic The record format version\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param baseOffset The starting offset\n     * @param logAppendTime The log append time\n     * @param producerId The producer's ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer's epoch\n     * @param baseSequence The starting sequence number\n     * @param public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n                logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, false, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a builder with control batch support.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Control Batches:</b> Used for transactional markers and coordination messages.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The destination {@link ByteBuffer}\n     * @param magic The record format version\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param timestampType The {@link TimestampType}\n     * @param baseOffset The starting offset\n     * @param logAppendTime The log append time\n     * @param producerId The producer's ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer's epoch\n     * @param baseSequence The starting sequence number\n     * @param isTransactional Whether records are transactional\n     * @param isControlBatch Whether this is a control batch\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @return A {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for appending records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional,\n                                               boolean isControlBatch,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n                logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlBatch, partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                buffer.remaining());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@code MemoryRecords} from simple records using default settings.\n     *\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return A {@code MemoryRecords} instance\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(Compression compression, SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withRecords(RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@code MemoryRecords} with partition leader epoch.\n     *\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return A {@code MemoryRecords} instance\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(Compression compression, int partitionLeaderEpoch, SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withRecords(RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, 0L, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE,\n                partitionLeaderEpoch, false, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@code MemoryRecords} with custom magic version.\n     *\n     * @param magic The record format version\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return A {@code MemoryRecords} instance\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(byte magic, Compression compression, SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withRecords(magic, 0L, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a {@code MemoryRecords} with custom base offset.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset The base offset for the first record\n     * @param compression The {@link Compression} algorithm\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return A {@code MemoryRecords}
